Avoid this place. Please read my comments below for reasons.

Short Story: Our insurance company is VSP. We received multiple confirmations from the front desk staff that "yes we are in network for VSP" before I start the eye exam and before I swipe my credit card. It turns out that they are not in network, and now they are playing dumb and insist on telling me to reach out to the insurance company to get reimbursed.

Long Story

We visited this store on 10/08/2020. Before we started the eye exam, they confirmed that my insurance works and should cover, so my wife and I went ahead and did the eye exam. The service seems to be pretty good, the doctor was patient in answering all my questions. However after we select the lenses and frames, we were told that they will charge the full amount without insurance adjustment, so that's over $2000 for both of us, and they will file claim forms to the insurance company for us so we can get reimbursed by the insurance company later. This makes me feel suspicious because the stores I visited in the last few years usually will directly calculate the amount that I should pay based on my insurance policy, rather than asking me for the full amount. So we asked again, "are you sure you are in network?" The front desk staff seems to be confused so she went inside and talked to the doctor, and came back telling us "yes we are in network", "no worries, you are covered". So I went ahead and made the purchase. Overall we think the service was pretty good so we even recommended this place to our friends.

On 10/29/2020, we went to the store to pick up the glasses. We were happy with the service so far and I ordered my second pair of glasses. Before I made the purchase, I asked again "are you sure you are really in network for VSP? this is a lot of money", the answer from the front desk staff was the same "yes we are in network". We left the store happily.

On 11/3/2020, we received the explanation of benefits from my insurance company. It states that the store is not in network so I'm only eligible for out of network coverage. I felt suspicious so I called the insurance company to confirm. The insurance company said ‚Äúthey are not in network. we can file a complaint for you as it seems that they lied to you about it, but unfortunately we cannot do anything else". I reached out to Eye Luv Lucy immediately, they pretended to not understand what I'm talking about and kept telling me to "talk to the insurance company to get what you are supposed to be reimbursed. Our job is already done." They don't pick up my phone calls any more. Luckily they have a number to receive messages so I can still send the messages.

On 11/6/2020, I sent messages indicating that if they don't offer a satisfactory solution, I might have to start writing negative reviews and think about going to court.

On 11/7/2020, I received a phone call from their manager. The manager was very reasonable. No one in our office claimed to promise that you paid zero even with with in network benefit. At this point, we can offer you credit toward 2 pairs of glasses that you paid forward as a courtesy‚Äù. Final words

<Name>Anonymous User</Name><Time>1521961338657</Time><Rate>1</Rate><review>New or potential clients beware!

It‚Äôs understandable that significant annual savings on health benefits motivate clients to migrate to Lumity however, after your initial year or two if you‚Äôre lucky, there will no longer be savings thus little to no incentive to stay. The trade-off for the dollars saved is potential compliance issues, on-going problems and lack of transparency related to your sensitive employee data, mediocre on-going client support, and little to no savings after your first year.

If you do not know yet, manual data manipulation is what powers Lumity. The Sales team will do a great job of selling you on future system functionality, but the reality is the product has not considerably changed in the last couple of years. You may be sold on EDI but it does not exist as management prefers to manually munge data. Unfortunately, system integrations and meaningful software releases move at a snail's pace as the engineering and product teams are bogged down with support/bug tickets and feature request to alleviate the administrative burden of the back office team.

When it comes to day-to-day support, the client services team is reactive instead of proactive and root cause analysis is used to identify a scapegoat rather than preventing issues long-term. The client service team will do a great job of making things ‚Äúhands-off‚Äù for their customers but this is mostly driven by the shortcomings of the product (i.e. Today, client administrators are not able to pull any reports including a simple employee census report from the admin portal). Unfortunately, there are some good account managers but they are not able to focus on more meaningful work for their customers as they are overwhelmed with escalations.

If you decide to on-board to Lumity be sure that your contract outlines the expectations which were discussed during the sales cycle.< /review>< Pics>
